{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"type":"text","text":"Base directory for this skill: /config/.claude/skills/sc-task-unified-protocol\n\n> **NOTE**: Classification has already been performed by the `/sc:task` command before this skill was invoked. The classification header has already been emitted. Do NOT emit it again. This skill handles **execution only** for STANDARD and STRICT tier tasks.\n>\n> If for any reason no classification header was emitted before this skill was invoked, emit one now using ONLY the tier values STRICT, STANDARD, LIGHT, or EXEMPT (no other values are valid).\n\n# /sc:task-unified - Unified Task Execution with Compliance\n\n## Purpose\n\nUnified command that merges orchestration capabilities with MCP compliance enforcement. Automatically classifies tasks into compliance tiers and enforces appropriate verification.\n\n**Key Benefits**:\n- Single command replaces confusion between `sc:task` and `sc:task-mcp`\n- Automatic tier classification with confidence scoring\n- Appropriate verification for each task type\n- Prevents over-engineering for trivial changes\n- Ensures safety for critical changes\n\n## Triggers\n\nUse `/sc:task` when:\n- Task involves code modifications with downstream impacts\n- Complexity score >0.6 with code modifications\n- Multi-file scope (>2 estimated affected files)\n- Security domain paths detected (auth/, security/, crypto/)\n- Refactoring or system-wide changes requested\n\n**Auto-Suggest Keywords**:\n- High confidence: \"implement feature\", \"refactor system\", \"fix security\", \"add authentication\", \"update database schema\"\n- Moderate confidence: \"add new\", \"create component\", \"update service\", \"modify API\"\n\n## Usage\n\n```bash\n/sc:task [description]                           # Auto-detect all dimensions\n/sc:task [description] --compliance strict       # Force STRICT tier\n/sc:task [description] --compliance light        # Force LIGHT tier\n/sc:task [description] --skip-compliance         # Bypass compliance (escape hatch)\n/sc:task [description] --verify auto             # Auto-select verification\n```\n\n## Behavioral Flow\n\n### 0. Classification (Already Performed)\n\nClassification was handled by the `/sc:task` command before this skill was invoked. The tier has been determined and the classification header has been emitted. Proceed directly to execution based on the classified tier.\n\n**Reference** — the tier keyword tables (for context only, do not re-classify):\n- **STRICT**: security, authentication, database, migration, refactor, breaking change, encrypt, token, session, oauth\n- **EXEMPT**: explain, search, commit, push, plan, discuss, brainstorm\n- **LIGHT**: typo, comment, whitespace, lint, docstring, formatting, minor\n- **STANDARD**: implement, add, create, update, fix, build, modify, change (default)\n\n### 2. Confidence Display (Human-Readable)\n\nAfter the mandatory classification header, show a human-readable summary:\n\n```\n**Tier: STANDARD** [████████░░] 80%\n\nClassified as STANDARD:\n- Keywords matched: add, implement\n- Confidence score: 0.78\n- Considered alternatives: STRICT (0.35)\n```\n\nIf confidence <70%, add prompt: \"⚠️ Low confidence. Override with: `--compliance [strict|standard|light|exempt]`\"\n\n**Note**: The machine-readable header (Section 0) is for telemetry/A/B testing. This human-readable display is for user understanding.\n\n### 3. Execution Phase\n\nExecute task according to tier requirements:\n\n**STRICT Execution**:\n1. Activate project (mcp__serena__activate_project)\n2. Verify git working directory clean (git status)\n3. Load codebase context (codebase-retrieval)\n4. Check relevant memories (list_memories -> read_memory)\n5. Identify all affected files and test files\n6. Make changes with full checklist\n7. Identify all files that import changed code\n8. Update all affected files\n9. Spawn verification agent (quality-engineer)\n10. Run comprehensive tests: `pytest [path] -v`\n11. Answer adversarial questions\n\n**STANDARD Execution**:\n1. Load context via codebase-retrieval\n2. Search downstream impacts (find_referencing_symbols OR grep)\n3. Make changes\n4. Run affected tests OR document manual verification\n5. Verify basic functionality\n\n**LIGHT Execution**:\n1. Quick scope check (files/lines within bounds)\n2. Make changes\n3. Quick sanity check (syntax valid, no obvious errors)\n4. Proceed with judgment\n\n**EXEMPT Execution**:\n1. Execute immediately\n2. No verification overhead\n\n### 4. Verification Phase\n\nRoute to appropriate verification based on tier and paths:\n\n| Compliance Tier | Verification Method | Token Cost | Timeout |\n|-----------------|---------------------|------------|---------|\n| STRICT | Sub-agent (quality-engineer) | 3-5K | 60s |\n| STANDARD | Direct test execution | 300-500 | 30s |\n| LIGHT | Skip verification | 0 | 0s |\n| EXEMPT | Skip verification | 0 | 0s |\n\n**Critical Path Override**: Paths matching `auth/`, `security/`, `crypto/`, `models/`, `migrations/` always trigger CRITICAL verification regardless of compliance tier.\n\n**Trivial Path Override**: Paths matching `*.md`, `docs/`, `*test*.py` may skip verification.\n\n### 4.5 Test Failure Escalation Protocol (TFEP)\n\n**CRITICAL**: When tests fail during the Verification Phase (Section 4), agents MUST follow this protocol. Ad-hoc fixes are PROHIBITED.\n\n#### TFEP Prohibition Rules (VIOLATION-level)\n\nThese rules apply to ALL compliance tiers that run tests (STRICT, STANDARD):\n\n1. **VIOLATION**: Agents MUST NOT fix any code in response to test failures without completing the TFEP workflow.\n2. **VIOLATION**: Agents MUST NOT modify test expectations to make failing tests pass without adversarial validation.\n3. **VIOLATION**: Ad-hoc patches derived from test output are PROHIBITED. The agent must not read a traceback and immediately edit code to resolve it.\n\n**Permitted Exceptions** (MAY fix directly without TFEP):\n- Single `ImportError`/`NameError` in test scaffolding the agent just wrote, affecting <=2 tests, where the error is in the test file itself (not in implementation code).\n- Lint/formatting failures (trivially fixable, unambiguous root cause).\n- Deprecation warnings (not failures).\n\n**Valid Adversarial Outcome**: \"Test expectations are wrong\" is a legitimate conclusion from adversarial debate. When the debate concludes that test expectations are outdated rather than the code being wrong, this is NOT grounds for the agent to directly edit the tests — it must be presented to the user for review.\n\n#### Test Baseline Snapshot (Pre-Implementation)\n\nBefore implementation begins, the agent MUST record a test baseline:\n\n1. Capture the list of all existing test files and test function names at task start (e.g., via `uv run pytest --collect-only -q` or directory listing).\n2. Store this baseline in memory for the duration of the task.\n3. On any test failure, classify each failing test as:\n   - **Pre-existing**: Test name appears in the baseline (existed before this task).\n   - **New**: Test name does NOT appear in the baseline (written by the agent during this task).\n4. This classification drives the MUST-escalate vs MAY-fix-directly decision below.\n\n#### Escalation Trigger Detection\n\n**MUST escalate (trigger TFEP):**\n- Any **pre-existing test** fails (tests in the baseline that were not modified by the agent). This is the primary trigger — regressions in existing tests indicate the implementation broke something.\n- **3 or more new tests** fail simultaneously (indicates a systemic issue, not a simple typo).\n- **Runtime exceptions in implementation code** (TypeError, AttributeError, KeyError, etc. in the code being tested, not in the test scaffolding itself).\n\n**Escalation gradient (within-TFEP, for future forensic integration):**\n- Repeated failure (same test cluster fails after fix attempt) → escalate from light to standard\n- Multi-file blast radius from recent changes → escalate\n- Low-confidence root cause from adversarial debate → escalate\n- Unresolved adversarial outcome (no winner/tie) → escalate\n- Second failed retest → escalate\n- Cross-domain or non-obvious regression → escalate\n\n#### TFEP Execution Flow\n\nWhen TFEP triggers, execute the following steps:\n\n**Step 1: Halt and freeze**\n1. **STOP** testing immediately.\n2. **FREEZE** implementation — no further code changes permitted.\n\n**Step 2: Construct failure context**\n3. Build a `failure_context` YAML package containing:\n   - `test_names`: list of failing test function names\n   - `test_files`: list of test files containing failures\n   - `error_output`: full traceback/error output\n   - `expected_behavior`: what was expected\n   - `actual_behavior`: what actually happened\n   - `changes_made`: files changed during this task with descriptions\n   - `task_description`: current task description\n   - `test_baseline`: the pre-implementation test baseline\n   - `escalation_count`: which TFEP trigger this is (1, 2, or 3)\n4. Write context to `{output_dir}/context.yaml`.\n\n**Step 3: Invoke forensic**\n5. Determine the forensic tier based on escalation count:\n   - 1st trigger → `--tier light --intent triage`\n   - 2nd trigger → `--tier standard`\n   - 3rd trigger → **FULL STOP**. Report to user. Do not attempt further fixes.\n6. Invoke: `/sc:forensic --tier {tier} --intent triage --caller task-unified --context {context_path} --output {output_dir} --depth quick`\n7. The forensic pipeline runs autonomously through all its phases and returns a structured return contract.\n\n**Step 4: Consume forensic results**\n8. Read the forensic return contract from `{output_dir}/return-contract.yaml`.\n9. Handle based on status:\n   - If `test_is_wrong == true`: Present to user for review. Do NOT auto-fix tests.\n   - If `status == \"success\"`: Proceed to Step 5 (tasklist insertion).\n   - If `status == \"partial\"` or `recommended_escalation != \"none\"`: Increment `escalation_count` and return to Step 3.\n   - If `status == \"failed\"`: Report to user, halt execution.\n\n**Step 5: Tasklist insertion**\n10. Read `tasklist_insertion_path` from the return contract.\n11. Insert the remediation block into the current tasklist:\n    - Add `## Failure Remediation Plan (Adjudicated)` heading.\n    - Insert remediation tasks BEFORE existing test/verification tasks.\n    - Preserve original tasklist structure — append, don't replace.\n\n**Step 6: Resume**\n12. Resume execution with `--compliance strict` starting from the inserted remediation tasks.\n13. After remediation tasks complete, re-run the original test suite.\n14. If tests pass: TFEP resolved successfully. Produce incident report and continue.\n15. If tests fail again: Increment `escalation_count`, return to Step 2.\n\n#### TFEP Incident Reporting\n\nAfter each TFEP resolution (success or escalation), produce `tfep-incident-report.md`:\n\n```markdown\n# TFEP Incident Report\n\n- **Trigger**: {which threshold rule fired}\n- **Escalation count**: {1, 2, or 3}\n- **Failing tests**: {test names and classification}\n- **Root cause**: {summary from rca-verdict.md}\n- **Solution**: {summary from solution-verdict.md}\n- **Outcome**: {success / escalated / failed}\n- **Forensic artifacts**: {path to output_dir}\n```\n\nThis report is committed to git alongside other forensic artifacts.\n\n#### Escalation Budget\n\n```\n1st TFEP trigger  → /sc:forensic --tier light --intent triage    (~5-8K tokens)\n2nd TFEP trigger  → /sc:forensic --tier standard                 (~15-20K tokens)\n3rd TFEP trigger  → FULL STOP. Report to user. Do not attempt further fixes.\n```\n\n### 5. Feedback Collection\n\nAfter completion, collect implicit feedback:\n- Track if user overrode tier (implicit classification feedback)\n- Note smooth completion vs errors (quality signal)\n- Store for calibration learning\n\n## MCP Integration\n\n**Required Servers by Tier**:\n- STRICT: Sequential, Serena (fallback not allowed)\n- STANDARD: Sequential, Context7 (fallback allowed)\n- LIGHT: None required (fallback allowed)\n- EXEMPT: None required\n\n**Circuit Breaker Behavior**:\n- If required servers unavailable for STRICT tier, block task execution\n- For other tiers, use fallbacks with noted limitations\n\n## Tool Coordination\n\n**Planning Phase**:\n1. TodoWrite: Create task breakdown\n2. codebase-retrieval: Load context\n3. list_memories / read_memory: Check project state\n\n**Execution Phase**:\n1. Edit/MultiEdit/Write: Make changes\n2. Grep/Glob: Find references\n3. find_referencing_symbols: Trace dependencies\n\n**Verification Phase**:\n1. Task (quality-engineer): Spawn verification agent (STRICT only)\n2. Bash: Run tests directly (STANDARD)\n3. think_about_task_adherence: Reflect on completeness\n\n**Completion Phase**:\n1. write_memory: Save session state\n2. think_about_whether_you_are_done: Final check\n\n## Examples\n\n### STRICT Task\n```\n/sc:task \"implement user authentication with JWT\"\n\n-> Classified as STRICT (security domain, authentication keyword)\n-> Full 6-category checklist enforced\n-> Verification agent spawned\n-> Adversarial questions answered\n```\n\n### STANDARD Task\n```\n/sc:task \"add pagination to user list\"\n\n-> Classified as STANDARD (add keyword, typical feature)\n-> Context loaded before editing\n-> Downstream impacts checked\n-> Direct test execution\n```\n\n### LIGHT Task\n```\n/sc:task \"fix typo in README\"\n\n-> Classified as LIGHT (trivial keyword, documentation path)\n-> Quick sanity check only\n-> No verification delay\n```\n\n### EXEMPT Task\n```\n/sc:task \"explain how the auth flow works\"\n\n-> Classified as EXEMPT (explain pattern detected)\n-> Immediate execution\n-> No compliance overhead\n```\n\n### Override Example\n```\n/sc:task \"update config file\" --compliance strict\n\n-> User override to STRICT regardless of classification\n-> Full verification enforced\n```\n\n## Boundaries\n\n**Will:**\n- Classify tasks into appropriate compliance tiers\n- Enforce tier-appropriate verification requirements\n- Provide confidence scoring with rationale\n- Track feedback for continuous calibration\n- Support user overrides with justification\n\n**Will Not:**\n- Skip safety-critical verification for STRICT tasks\n- Apply STRICT overhead to genuinely trivial changes\n- Override user's explicit compliance choice\n- Proceed with <70% confidence without user confirmation\n\n## Success Criteria\n\n| Metric | Target | Measurement |\n|--------|--------|-------------|\n| Tier classification accuracy | >=80% | User feedback on appropriateness |\n| User confusion rate | <10% | \"Which command?\" questions eliminated \"\\n\".join(lines) + \"\\n\"\n   295→\n   296→\n   297→def aggregate_task_results(\n   298→    phase_number: int,\n   299→    task_results: list[TaskResult],\n   300→    remaining_task_ids: list[str] | None = None,\n   301→    budget_remaining: int = 0,\n   302→) -> AggregatedPhaseReport:\n   303→    \"\"\"Aggregate individual TaskResults into a runner-constructed PhaseReport.\n   304→\n   305→    This function is the runner's authoritative source of task outcomes.\n   306→    It does not rely on agent self-reporting.\n   307→\n   308→    Args:\n   309→        phase_number: The phase number being aggregated.\n   310→        task_results: List of TaskResult from execute_phase_tasks().\n   311→        remaining_task_ids: Task IDs that were not attempted due to budget.\n   312→\n   313→    Returns:\n   314→        AggregatedPhaseReport with computed counts and status.\n   315→    \"\"\"\n   316→    report = AggregatedPhaseReport(\n   317→        phase_number=phase_number,\n   318→        task_results=task_results,\n   319→        remaining_task_ids=remaining_task_ids or [],\n   320→        budget_remaining=budget_remaining,\n   321→    )\n   322→\n   323→    report.tasks_total = len(task_results) + len(report.remaining_task_ids)\n   324→    report.tasks_passed = sum(1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.PASS)\n   325→    report.tasks_failed = sum(1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.FAIL)\n   326→    report.tasks_incomplete = sum(\n   327→        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n   328→    )\n   329→    report.tasks_skipped = sum(\n   330→        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.SKIPPED\n   331→    )\n   332→    report.tasks_not_attempted = len(report.remaining_task_ids)\n   333→    report.total_turns_consumed = sum(r.turns_consumed for r in task_results)\n   334→    report.total_duration_seconds = sum(r.duration_seconds for r in task_results)\n   335→\n   336→    return report\n   337→\n   338→\n   339→def check_budget_guard(ledger: TurnLedger | None) -> str | None:\n   340→    \"\"\"Pre-launch budget guard: returns a halt message if budget is insufficient.\n   341→\n   342→    Returns None if launch is allowed, or a descriptive message string\n   343→    if the budget is too low to launch a subprocess.\n   344→    \"\"\"\n   345→    if ledger is None:\n   346→        return None\n   347→    if ledger.can_launch():\n   348→        return None\n   349→    return (\n   350→        f\"Budget exhausted: {ledger.available()} turns remaining, \"\n   351→        f\"minimum {ledger.minimum_allocation} required for launch\"\n   352→    )\n   353→\n   354→\n   355→def run_wiring_safeguard_checks(\n   356→    config: SprintConfig,\n   357→    report: object | None = None,\n   358→) -> list[str]:\n   359→    \"\"\"Pre-activation safeguards for wiring analysis (SC-010, section 7 Phase 1).\n   360→\n   361→    Checks run before the first wiring analysis in a sprint session:\n   362→    1. Zero-match warning: >50 files scanned but 0 findings → suspicious\n   363→    2. Whitelist validation: attempt to load whitelist, warn if parse fails\n   364→    3. provider_dir_names check: verify configured directories exist\n   365→\n   366→    Safeguards produce warnings only; they never block sprint execution.\n   367→\n   368→    Returns a list of warning messages (empty if all checks pass).\n   369→    \"\"\"\n   370→    from superclaude.cli.audit.wiring_config import WiringConfig, load_whitelist\n   371→\n   372→    warnings: list[str] = []\n   373→\n   374→    # Check 1: Zero-match warning (requires a report from a prior run)\n   375→    if report is not None:\n   376→        files_scanned = getattr(report, \"files_analyzed\", 0)\n   377→        total_findings = getattr(report, \"total_findings\", 0)\n   378→        if files_scanned > 50 and total_findings == 0:\n   379→            msg = (\n   380→                f\"Zero-match warning: {files_scanned} files scanned but \"\n   381→                f\"0 findings produced — verify wiring analysis configuration\"\n   382→            )\n   383→            _wiring_logger.warning(msg)\n   384→            warnings.append(msg)\n   385→\n   386→    # Check 2: Whitelist validation\n   387→    # Try to parse with \"soft\" mode so malformed YAML raises instead of silently\n   388→    # returning empty. This is a safeguard check, not runtime behavior.\n   389→    whitelist_path = config.release_dir / \"src\" / \"superclaude\" / \"cli\" / \"audit\" / \"wiring_whitelist.yaml\"\n   390→    if whitelist_path.exists():\n   391→        try:\n   392→            import yaml as _yaml\n   393→            raw = _yaml.safe_load(whitelist_path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\"))\n   394→            if not isinstance(raw, dict):\n   395→                msg = f\"Whitelist validation failed: file at {whitelist_path} is not a YAML mapping\"\n   396→                _wiring_logger.warning(msg)\n   397→                warnings.append(msg)\n   398→        except Exception as exc:\n   399→            msg = f\"Whitelist validation failed: {exc}\"\n   400→            _wiring_logger.warning(msg)\n   401→            warnings.append(msg)\n   402→\n   403→    # Check 3: provider_dir_names sanity check\n   404→    wiring_config = WiringConfig()\n   405→    source_dir = config.release_dir\n   406→    for dir_name in wiring_config.provider_dir_names:\n   407→        found = list(source_dir.rglob(dir_name))\n   408→        dirs_found = [d for d in found if d.is_dir()]\n   409→        if not dirs_found:\n   410→            msg = (\n   411→                f\"Provider directory '{dir_name}' not found under \"\n   412→                f\"{source_dir} — orphan module detection may miss files\"\n   413→            )\n   414→            _wiring_logger.warning(msg)\n   415→            warnings.append(msg)\n   416→\n   417→    return warnings\n   418→\n   419→\n   420→def _resolve_wiring_mode(config: SprintConfig) -> str:\n   421→    \"\"\"Resolve the effective wiring gate mode from config.\n   422→\n   423→    Uses resolve_gate_mode(scope, grace_period) from trailing_gate.py\n   424→    to map scope-based configuration to an effective mode string (Goal-5d).\n   425→    Falls back to config.wiring_gate_mode if scope resolution is not applicable.\n   426→    \"\"\"\n   427→    from superclaude.cli.pipeline.trailing_gate import GateScope, resolve_gate_mode\n   428→    from superclaude.cli.pipeline.models import GateMode\n   429→\n   430→    scope_map = {\n   431→        \"release\": GateScope.RELEASE,\n   432→        \"milestone\": GateScope.MILESTONE,\n   433→        \"task\": GateScope.TASK,\n   434→    }\n   435→    scope = scope_map.get(config.wiring_gate_scope)\n   436→    if scope is None:\n   437→        return config.wiring_gate_mode\n   438→\n   439→    gate_mode = resolve_gate_mode(scope=scope, grace_period=0)\n   440→\n   441→    # Map GateMode back to wiring mode string\n   442→    mode_map = {\n   443→        GateMode.BLOCKING: \"full\",\n   444→        GateMode.TRAILING: \"shadow\",\n   445→    }\n   446→    return mode_map.get(gate_mode, config.wiring_gate_mode)\n   447→\n   448→\n   449→def run_post_task_wiring_hook(\n   450→    task: TaskEntry,\n   451→    config: SprintConfig,\n   452→    task_result: TaskResult,\n   453→    ledger: TurnLedger | None = None,\n   454→) -> TaskResult:\n   455→    \"\"\"Run post-task wiring analysis based on config.wiring_gate_mode.\n   456→\n   457→    Integrates with TurnLedger for budget-aware gate enforcement:\n   458→    - Checks can_run_wiring_gate() before analysis (debit-before-analysis)\n   459→    - Uses resolve_gate_mode(scope, grace_period) for mode resolution (Goal-5d)\n   460→    - Callable-based remediation interface avoids TurnLedger import in\n   461→      trailing_gate.py (Constraint 7)\n   462→\n   463→    Mode behavior:\n   464→    - off: skip analysis entirely, return task_result unchanged\n   465→    - shadow: run analysis, log findings, task status unchanged (SC-006)\n   466→    - soft: run analysis, warn on critical findings, task status unchanged\n   467→    - full: run analysis, block (set FAIL) on critical+major findings,\n   468→            invoke remediation via callable interface\n   469→\n   470→    Returns the (possibly modified) TaskResult. Only full mode may change\n   471→    task status to FAIL when blocking findings exist.\n   472→    \"\"\"\n   473→    mode = config.wiring_gate_mode\n   474→\n   475→    if mode == \"off\":\n   476→        return task_result\n   477→\n   478→    # Budget guard: check if wiring analysis budget allows this run\n   479→    if ledger is not None and not ledger.can_run_wiring_gate():\n   480→        _wiring_logger.info(\n   481→            \"Wiring hook skipped for task %s: budget exhausted\",\n   482→            task.task_id,\n   483→        )\n   484→        return task_result\n   485→\n   486→    # Debit wiring turns before analysis (debit-before-analysis model)\n   487→    if ledger is not None:\n   488→        ledger.debit_wiring(config.wiring_analysis_turns)\n   489→\n   490→    # Lazy import to avoid circular dependency at module level\n   491→    from superclaude.cli.audit.wiring_gate import run_wiring_analysis, WiringReport\n   492→    from superclaude.cli.audit.wiring_config import WiringConfig\n   493→\n   494→    source_dir = config.release_dir\n   495→    wiring_config = WiringConfig(rollout_mode=mode if mode in (\"shadow\", \"soft\", \"full\") else \"shadow\")\n   496→\n   497→    try:\n   498→        report = run_wiring_analysis(wiring_config, source_dir)\n   499→    except Exception as exc:\n   500→        _wiring_logger.warning(\n   501→            \"Wiring analysis failed for task %s: %s — continuing\",\n   502→            task.task_id,\n   503→            exc,\n   504→        )\n   505→        return task_result\n   506→\n   507→    total = report.total_findings\n   508→    blocking = report.blocking_count(mode)\n   509→\n   510→    _wiring_logger.info(\n   511→        \"Wiring hook [%s] task=%s: %d findings, %d blocking (%.4fs)\",\n   512→        mode,\n   513→        task.task_id,\n   514→        total,\n   515→        blocking,\n   516→        report.scan_duration_seconds,\n   517→    )\n   518→\n   519→    if mode == \"shadow\":\n   520→        # SC-006: log findings without affecting task status\n   521→        if total > 0:\n   522→            _wiring_logger.info(\n   523→                \"Shadow mode: %d findings logged for task %s (status unchanged)\",\n   524→                total,\n   525→                task.task_id,\n   526→            )\n   527→        # Credit wiring turns back (shadow never blocks)\n   528→        if ledger is not None:\n   529→            ledger.credit_wiring(config.wiring_analysis_turns)\n   530→        return task_result\n   531→\n   532→    if mode == \"soft\":\n   533→        # Warn on critical findings but don't change status\n   534→        critical_count = sum(\n   535→            1 for f in report.unsuppressed_findings if f.severity == \"critical\"\n   536→        )\n   537→        if critical_count > 0:\n   538→            _wiring_logger.warning(\n   539→                \"Soft mode: %d critical findings for task %s\",\n   540→                critical_count,\n   541→                task.task_id,\n   542→            )\n   543→        # Credit wiring turns back (soft never blocks)\n   544→        if ledger is not None:\n   545→            ledger.credit_wiring(config.wiring_analysis_turns)\n   546→        return task_result\n   547→\n   548→    if mode == \"full\":\n   549→        # Block on critical+major findings\n   550→        if blocking > 0:\n   551→            _wiring_logger.error(\n   552→                \"Full mode: %d blocking findings for task %s — marking FAIL\",\n   553→                blocking,\n   554→                task.task_id,\n   555→            )\n   556→            task_result.status = TaskStatus.FAIL\n   557→            task_result.gate_outcome = GateOutcome.FAIL\n   558→\n   559→            # Remediation via callable interface (Constraint 7)\n   560→            # Pass TurnLedger methods as callables to avoid import coupling\n   561→            if ledger is not None:\n   562→                can_remediate = ledger.can_remediate\n   563→                debit = lambda turns: ledger.debit(turns)  # noqa: E731\n   564→                if can_remediate():\n   565→                    debit(config.remediation_cost)\n   566→                    _wiring_logger.info(\n   567→                        \"Full mode: remediation debited %d turns for task %s\",\n   568→                        config.remediation_cost,\n   569→                        task.task_id,\n   570→                    )\n   571→                else:\n   572→                    _wiring_logger.warning(\n   573→                        \"Full mode: BUDGET_EXHAUSTED for task %s remediation\",\n   574→                        task.task_id,\n   575→                    )\n   576→        else:\n   577→            # No blocking findings — credit turns back\n   578→            if ledger is not None:\n   579→                ledger.credit_wiring(config.wiring_analysis_turns)\n   580→        return task_result\n   581→\n   582→    return task_result\n   583→\n   584→\n   585→def run_post_task_anti_instinct_hook(\n   586→    task: TaskEntry,\n   587→    config: SprintConfig,\n   588→    task_result: TaskResult,\n   589→    ledger: TurnLedger | None = None,\n   590→    shadow_metrics: ShadowGateMetrics | None = None,\n   591→) -> TaskResult:\n   592→    \"\"\"Run post-task anti-instinct gate based on config.gate_rollout_mode.\n   593→\n   594→    Mode behavior matrix:\n   595→    - off: evaluate gate, ignore result (metrics not recorded)\n   596→    - shadow: evaluate gate, record metrics via ShadowGateMetrics (FR-SPRINT.4)\n   597→    - soft: evaluate + record + credit on PASS / remediate on FAIL (FR-SPRINT.3)\n   598→    - full: evaluate + record + credit on PASS / remediate on FAIL / set FAIL status (FR-SPRINT.3)\n   599→\n   600→    All TurnLedger calls are guarded with ``if ledger is not None`` (NFR-007).\n   601→    Anti-instinct and wiring-integrity gates evaluate independently (NFR-010).\n   602→\n   603→    Returns the (possibly modified) TaskResult.\n   604→    \"\"\"\n   605→    import math\n   606→    import time as _time\n   607→\n   608→    mode = config.gate_rollout_mode\n   609→\n   610→    if mode == \"off\":\n   611→        # Evaluate but ignore — no metrics, no side effects\n   612→        return task_result\n   613→\n   614→    # Lazy import to avoid circular dependency\n   615→    from superclaude.cli.pipeline.gates import gate_passed\n   616→    from superclaude.cli.roadmap.gates import ANTI_INSTINCT_GATE\n   617→\n   618→    # Evaluate the anti-instinct gate on the task's output artifact\n   619→    output_path = Path(task_result.output_path) if task_result.output_path else None\n   620→\n   621→    eval_start = _time.monotonic()\n   622→    if output_path is not None and output_path.exists():\n   623→        passed, failure_reason = gate_passed(output_path, ANTI_INSTINCT_GATE)\n   624→    else:\n   625→        # No output artifact to evaluate — gate passes vacuously\n   626→        passed = True\n   627→        failure_reason = None\n   628→    eval_end = _time.monotonic()\n   629→    evaluation_ms = (eval_end - eval_start) * 1000.0\n   630→\n   631→    _anti_instinct_logger.info(\n   632→        \"Anti-instinct hook [%s] task=%s: passed=%s (%.1fms)\",\n   633→        mode,\n   634→        task.task_id,\n   635→        passed,\n   636→        evaluation_ms,\n   637→    )\n   638→\n   639→    # Record metrics for shadow/soft/full modes (FR-SPRINT.4)\n   640→    if shadow_metrics is not None:\n   641→        shadow_metrics.record(passed=passed, evaluation_ms=evaluation_ms)\n   642→\n   643→    if mode == \"shadow\":\n   644→        # Record metrics only, no behavioral impact\n   645→        return task_result\n   646→\n   647→    # soft and full modes: credit on PASS, remediate on FAIL\n   648→    if passed:\n   649→        # Credit path: reimburse turns on gate PASS\n   650→        if ledger is not None:\n   651→            credit_amount = int(task_result.turns_consumed * ledger.reimbursement_rate)\n   652→            ledger.credit(credit_amount)\n   653→            task_result.reimbursement_amount = credit_amount\n   654→            _anti_instinct_logger.info(\n   655→                \"Anti-instinct PASS: credited %d turns for task %s\",\n   656→                credit_amount,\n   657→                task.task_id,\n   658→            )\n   659→        task_result.gate_outcome = GateOutcome.PASS\n   660→    else:\n   661→        # Remediation path: check budget, mark BUDGET_EXHAUSTED or FAIL\n   662→        if ledger is not None and not ledger.can_remediate():\n   663→            _anti_instinct_logger.warning(\n   664→                \"Anti-instinct FAIL + BUDGET_EXHAUSTED for task %s: \"\n   665→                \"available=%d < minimum_remediation_budget=%d\",\n   666→                task.task_id,\n   667→                ledger.available(),\n   668→                ledger.minimum_remediation_budget,\n   669→            )\n   670→            task_result.gate_outcome = GateOutcome.FAIL\n   671→            if mode == \"full\":\n   672→                task_result.status = TaskStatus.FAIL\n   673→            return task_result\n   674→\n   675→        _anti_instinct_logger.warning(\n   676→            \"Anti-instinct FAIL for task %s: %s\",\n   677→            task.task_id,\n   678→            failure_reason or \"unknown reason\",\n   679→        )\n   680→        task_result.gate_outcome = GateOutcome.FAIL\n   681→\n   682→        if mode == \"full\":\n   683→            # Full mode: fail the task\n   684→            task_result.status = TaskStatus.FAIL\n   685→\n   686→    return task_result\n   687→\n   688→\n   689→def execute_phase_tasks(\n   690→    tasks: list[TaskEntry],\n   691→    config: SprintConfig,\n   692→    phase,\n   693→    ledger: TurnLedger | None = None,\n   694→    *,\n   695→    _subprocess_factory=None,\n   696→    shadow_metrics: ShadowGateMetrics | None = None,\n   697→) -> tuple[list[TaskResult], list[str]]:\n   698→    \"\"\"Per-task subprocess orchestration loop.\n   699→\n   700→    Iterates over a task inventory, spawning one subprocess per task with\n   701→    budget allocation from the TurnLedger. Returns task results and a list\n   702→    of remaining (unattempted) task IDs if budget was exhausted.\n   703→\n   704→    Args:\n   705→        tasks: Ordered list of TaskEntry from the tasklist parser.\n   706→        config: Sprint configuration.\n   707→        phase: The Phase being executed.\n   708→        ledger: Optional TurnLedger for budget tracking.\n   709→        _subprocess_factory: Optional callable for testing; signature\n   710→            ``(task, config, phase) -> (exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes)``.\n   711→        shadow_metrics: Optional ShadowGateMetrics for anti-instinct gate\n   712→            metrics collection (used in shadow/soft/full rollout modes).\n   713→\n   714→    Returns:\n   715→        Tuple of (results, remaining_task_ids). remaining_task_ids is non-empty\n   716→        only when the loop halted due to budget exhaustion.\n   717→    \"\"\"\n   718→    results: list[TaskResult] = []\n   719→    remaining: list[str] = []\n   720→\n   721→    if not tasks:\n   722→        return results, remaining\n   723→\n   724→    for i, task in enumerate(tasks):\n   725→        started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   726→\n   727→        # Budget check: can we launch?\n   728→        if ledger is not None and not ledger.can_launch():\n   729→            # Mark this and all subsequent tasks as skipped\n   730→            remaining = [t.task_id for t in tasks[i:]]\n   731→            for t in tasks[i:]:\n   732→                results.append(\n   733→                    TaskResult(\n   734→                        task=t,\n   735→                        status=TaskStatus.SKIPPED,\n   736→                        started_at=started_at,\n   737→                        finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n   738→                    )\n   739→                )\n   740→            break\n   741→\n   742→        # Debit the minimum allocation upfront\n   743→        if ledger is not None:\n   744→            ledger.debit(ledger.minimum_allocation)\n   745→\n   746→        # Spawn subprocess for this task\n   747→        if _subprocess_factory is not None:\n   748→            exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes = _subprocess_factory(\n   749→                task, config, phase\n   750→            )\n   751→        else:\n   752→            # Default: delegate to ClaudeProcess (real execution)\n   753→            exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes = _run_task_subprocess(\n   754→                task, config, phase\n   755→            )\n   756→\n   757→        finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   758→\n   759→        # Determine task status from exit code\n   760→        if exit_code == 0:\n   761→            status = TaskStatus.PASS\n   762→        elif exit_code == 124:\n   763→            status = TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n   764→        else:\n   765→            status = TaskStatus.FAIL\n   766→\n   767→        # Reconcile budget: debit actual consumption, credit back pre-allocation\n   768→        if ledger is not None:\n   769→            # We pre-debited minimum_allocation; now adjust for actual turns\n   770→            actual = max(turns_consumed, 0)\n   771→            pre_allocated = ledger.minimum_allocation\n   772→            if actual > pre_allocated:\n   773→                ledger.debit(actual - pre_allocated)\n   774→            elif actual < pre_allocated:\n   775→                ledger.credit(pre_allocated - actual)\n   776→\n   777→        result = TaskResult(\n   778→            task=task,\n   779→            status=status,\n   780→            turns_consumed=turns_consumed,\n   781→            exit_code=exit_code,\n   782→            started_at=started_at,\n   783→            finished_at=finished_at,\n   784→            output_bytes=output_bytes,\n   785→        )\n   786→\n   787→        # Post-task wiring hook: run wiring analysis per config.wiring_gate_mode\n   788→        result = run_post_task_wiring_hook(task, config, result, ledger=ledger)\n   789→\n   790→        # Post-task anti-instinct hook: run anti-instinct gate per config.gate_rollout_mode\n   791→        # NFR-010: anti-instinct and wiring gates evaluate independently (no shared state)\n   792→        result = run_post_task_anti_instinct_hook(\n   793→            task, config, result, ledger=ledger, shadow_metrics=shadow_metrics,\n   794→        )\n   795→\n   796→        results.append(result)\n   797→\n   798→    return results, remaining\n   799→\n   800→\n   801→def _run_task_subprocess(\n   802→    task: TaskEntry,\n   803→    config: SprintConfig,\n   804→    phase,\n   805→) -> tuple[int, int, int]:\n   806→    \"\"\"Run a single task in a subprocess. Returns (exit_code, turns, output_bytes).\n   807→\n   808→    This is the real implementation that spawns a ClaudeProcess. For testing,\n   809→    callers of execute_phase_tasks pass _subprocess_factory instead.\n   810→    \"\"\"\n   811→    # Build a task-specific prompt\n   812→    prompt = (\n   813→        f\"Execute task {task.task_id}: {task.title}\\n\"\n   814→        f\"From phase file: {phase.file}\\n\"\n   815→        f\"Description: {task.description}\\n\"\n   816→    )\n   817→\n   818→    proc = ClaudeProcess.__new__(ClaudeProcess)\n   819→    proc.config = config\n   820→    proc.phase = phase\n   821→    from superclaude.cli.pipeline.process import ClaudeProcess as _Base\n   822→\n   823→    _Base.__init__(\n   824→        proc,\n   825→        prompt=prompt,\n   826→        output_file=config.output_file(phase),\n   827→        error_file=config.error_file(phase),\n   828→        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n   829→        model=config.model,\n   830→        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n   831→        timeout_seconds=config.max_turns * 120 + 300,\n   832→        output_format=\"stream-json\",\n   833→    )\n   834→    proc.start()\n   835→    proc.wait()\n   836→    exit_code = proc._process.returncode if proc._process else -1\n   837→    output_path = config.output_file(phase)\n   838→    output_bytes = output_path.stat().st_size if output_path.exists() else 0\n   839→    # Turn counting is wired separately in T02.06\n   840→    return (exit_code if exit_code is not None else -1, 0, output_bytes)\n   841→\n   842→\n   843→def execute_sprint(config: SprintConfig):\n   844→    \"\"\"Main orchestration loop.\n   845→\n   846→    For each active phase:\n   847→    1. Launch claude -p subprocess\n   848→    2. Start output monitor thread\n   849→    3. Update TUI in a polling loop until process exits (with timeout)\n   850→    4. Parse result file for CONTINUE/HALT\n   851→    5. Record PhaseResult\n   852→    6. Decide whether to continue or halt\n   853→    \"\"\"\n   854→    # Pre-flight: verify claude binary is available before starting TUI/logging\n   855→    if shutil.which(\"claude\") is None:\n   856→        raise SystemExit(\n   857→            \"Error: 'claude' binary not found in PATH. \"\n   858→            \"Install Claude Code CLI before running sprint.\"\n   859→        )\n   860→\n   861→    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n   862→    signal_handler.install()\n   863→\n   864→    setup_debug_logger(config)\n   865→    import logging as _logging\n   866→\n   867→    _dbg = _logging.getLogger(_DBG_NAME)\n   868→\n   869→    logger = SprintLogger(config)\n   870→    tui = SprintTUI(config)\n   871→    monitor = OutputMonitor(Path(\"/dev/null\"))  # reset per phase\n   872→    proc_manager: ClaudeProcess | None = None\n   873→\n   874→    sprint_result = SprintResult(config=config)\n   875→    logger.write_header(sprint_result)\n   876→\n   877→    tui.start()\n   878→\n   879→    # Startup orphan cleanup: remove stale isolation dirs from crashed previous runs\n   880→    shutil.rmtree(config.results_dir / \".isolation\", ignore_errors=True)\n   881→\n   882→    # Execute all python-mode phases via preflight executor before the main loop.\n   883→    # Removing this single call reverts to all-Claude behavior (R-051 rollback property).\n   884→    # Lazy import breaks the preflight → executor → preflight circular import cycle.\n   885→    from .preflight import execute_preflight_phases  # noqa: PLC0415\n   886→\n   887→    preflight_results = execute_preflight_phases(config)\n   888→\n   889→    try:\n   890→        for phase in config.active_phases:\n   891→            if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n   892→                sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n   893→                break\n   894→\n   895→            # Python-mode phases were already executed by preflight; skip here.\n   896→            if phase.execution_mode == \"python\":\n   897→                continue\n   898→\n   899→            # Skip-mode phases: record SKIPPED with no subprocess launched.\n   900→            if phase.execution_mode == \"skip\":\n   901→                _now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   902→                skip_result = PhaseResult(\n   903→                    phase=phase,\n   904→                    status=PhaseStatus.SKIPPED,\n   905→                    exit_code=0,\n   906→                    started_at=_now,\n   907→                    finished_at=_now,\n   908→                )\n   909→                sprint_result.phase_results.append(skip_result)\n   910→                logger.write_phase_result(skip_result)\n   911→                continue\n   912→\n   913→            # Per-phase isolation directory: exactly one file (the phase file)\n   914→            isolation_dir = config.results_dir / \".isolation\" / f\"phase-{phase.number}\"\n   915→            isolation_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n   916→            shutil.copy2(phase.file, isolation_dir / phase.file.name)\n   917→\n   918→            try:\n   919→                # Reset monitor for this phase\n   920→                output_path = config.output_file(phase)\n   921→                monitor.reset(output_path)\n   922→                monitor.start()\n   923→\n   924→                # Update tmux tail pane if running in tmux\n   925→                if config.tmux_session_name:\n   926→                    update_tail_pane(config.tmux_session_name, output_path)\n   927→\n   928→                # Launch claude with isolation env vars (CLAUDE_WORK_DIR → isolation_dir)\n   929→                _phase_env_vars = {\n   930→                    \"CLAUDE_WORK_DIR\": str(isolation_dir),\n   931→                }\n   932→                proc_manager = ClaudeProcess(config, phase, env_vars=_phase_env_vars)\n   933→                proc_manager.start()\n   934→                started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   935→                # Use monotonic clock for deadline enforcement to be immune to NTP adjustments\n   936→                deadline = time.monotonic() + proc_manager.timeout_seconds\n   937→                logger.write_phase_start(phase, started_at)\n   938→\n   939→                debug_log(_dbg, \"PHASE_BEGIN\", phase=phase.number, file=str(phase.file))\n   940→\n   941→                tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, phase)\n   942→\n   943→                # Poll loop: wait for process to finish while updating TUI\n   944→                # Enforces monotonic timeout via deadline check.\n   945→                _timed_out = False\n   946→                _stall_acted = False  # single-fire guard for watchdog\n   947→                _poll_start = time.monotonic()\n   948→                while proc_manager._process.poll() is None:\n   949→                    if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n   950→                        proc_manager.terminate()\n   951→                        break\n   952→                    if time.monotonic() > deadline:\n   953→                        # Timeout reached: kill the process, exit loop\n   954→                        _timed_out = True\n   955→                        proc_manager.terminate()\n   956→                        break\n   957→\n   958→                    ms = monitor.state\n   959→                    _elapsed = time.monotonic() - _poll_start\n   960→\n   961→                    debug_log(\n   962→                        _dbg,\n   963→                        \"poll_tick\",\n   964→                        phase=phase.number,\n   965→                        pid=proc_manager._process.pid,\n   966→                        poll_result=\"running\",\n   967→                        elapsed=round(_elapsed, 1),\n   968→                        output_bytes=ms.output_bytes,\n   969→                        growth_rate=round(ms.growth_rate_bps, 1),\n   970→                        stall_seconds=round(ms.stall_seconds, 1),\n   971→                        stall_status=ms.stall_status,\n   972→                    )\n   973→\n   974→                    # --- Watchdog: stall timeout check ---\n   975→                    if (\n   976→                        config.stall_timeout > 0\n   977→                        and ms.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout\n   978→                        and ms.events_received > 0  # don't trigger during startup\n   979→                        and not _stall_acted\n   980→                    ):\n   981→                        _stall_acted = True\n   982→                        debug_log(\n   983→                            _dbg,\n   984→                            \"watchdog_triggered\",\n   985→                            phase=phase.number,\n   986→                            action=config.stall_action,\n   987→                            stall_seconds=round(ms.stall_seconds, 1),\n   988→                            pid=proc_manager._process.pid,\n   989→                        )\n   990→                        if config.stall_action == \"kill\":\n   991→                            import sys\n   992→\n   993→                            print(\n   994→                                f\"[WATCHDOG] Stall detected ({ms.stall_seconds:.0f}s > \"\n   995→                                f\"{config.stall_timeout}s) — killing phase {phase.number}\",\n   996→                                file=sys.stderr,\n   997→                            )\n   998→                            _timed_out = True\n   999→                            proc_manager.terminate()\n  1000→                            break\n  1001→                        else:\n  1002→                            # warn action: log and continue\n  1003→                            import sys\n  1004→\n  1005→                            print(\n  1006→                                f\"[WATCHDOG] Stall detected ({ms.stall_seconds:.0f}s > \"\n  1007→                                f\"{config.stall_timeout}s) — warning for phase {phase.number}\",\n  1008→                                file=sys.stderr,\n  1009→                            )\n  1010→\n  1011→                    # Reset single-fire guard when output resumes\n  1012→                    if _stall_acted and ms.stall_seconds == 0.0:\n  1013→                        _stall_acted = False\n  1014→\n  1015→                    # Update TUI at ~2 Hz (monitor thread handles data extraction)\n  1016→                    # Wrap in try/except so a display glitch cannot abort the sprint\n  1017→                    try:\n  1018→                        tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, phase)\n  1019→                    except Exception as _tui_exc:\n  1020→                        import sys\n  1021→\n  1022→                        print(\n  1023→                            f\"[TUI] Display error (continuing sprint): {_tui_exc}\",\n  1024→                            file=sys.stderr,\n  1025→                        )\n  1026→                    time.sleep(0.5)\n  1027→\n  1028→                # Safely read exit code: returncode may be None if terminate raced.\n  1029→                # Use _timed_out flag instead of assigning directly to returncode.\n  1030→                raw_rc = proc_manager._process.returncode\n  1031→                if _timed_out:\n  1032→                    exit_code = 124\n  1033→                else:\n  1034→                    exit_code = raw_rc if raw_rc is not None else -1\n  1035→                monitor.stop()\n  1036→                finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n  1037→                _phase_dur = (finished_at - started_at).total_seconds()\n  1038→                debug_log(\n  1039→                    _dbg,\n  1040→                    \"PHASE_END\",\n  1041→                    phase=phase.number,\n  1042→                    exit_code=exit_code,\n  1043→                    duration=round(_phase_dur, 1),\n  1044→                )\n  1045→\n  1046→                # If shutdown was requested during the poll loop, classify as\n  1047→                # INTERRUPTED rather than letting _determine_phase_status see\n  1048→                # exit_code=-1 (None→-1 fallback) and return PhaseStatus.ERROR,\n  1049→                # which would incorrectly set the outcome to HALTED.\n  1050→                if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n  1051→                    logger.write_phase_interrupt(\n  1052→                        phase, started_at, finished_at, exit_code\n  1053→                    )\n  1054→                    sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n  1055→                    break\n  1056→\n  1057→                # Write a preliminary result sentinel so _determine_phase_status()\n  1058→                # always finds a result file for exit_code=0 phases that wrote no report.\n  1059→                # Guard: only for successful exits; non-zero paths must not reach this.\n  1060→                if exit_code == 0:\n  1061→                    _wrote_preliminary = _write_preliminary_result(\n  1062→                        config, phase, started_at.timestamp()\n  1063→                    )\n  1064→                    debug_log(\n  1065→                        _dbg,\n  1066→                        \"preliminary_result_write\",\n  1067→                        path=f\"{'executor-preliminary (option_d)' if _wrote_preliminary else 'agent-written/option_a_or_noop'}\",\n  1068→                    )\n  1069→\n  1070→                # Determine phase status\n  1071→                status = _determine_phase_status(\n  1072→                    exit_code=exit_code,\n  1073→                    result_file=config.result_file(phase),\n  1074→                    output_file=config.output_file(phase),\n  1075→                    config=config,\n  1076→                    phase=phase,\n  1077→                    started_at=started_at.timestamp(),\n  1078→                    error_file=config.error_file(phase),\n  1079→                )\n  1080→\n  1081→                # Write executor result file for downstream consumers.\n  1082→                # Written AFTER status determination to avoid circularity.\n  1083→                # Overwrites any agent-written file — executor is authoritative.\n  1084→                _write_executor_result_file(\n  1085→                    config=config,\n  1086→                    phase=phase,\n  1087→                    status=status,\n  1088→                    exit_code=exit_code,\n  1089→                    monitor_state=monitor.state,\n  1090→                    started_at=started_at,\n  1091→                    finished_at=finished_at,\n  1092→                )\n  1093→\n  1094→                # Collect stderr size for telemetry\n  1095→                error_file = config.error_file(phase)\n  1096→                error_bytes = error_file.stat().st_size if error_file.exists() else 0\n  1097→\n  1098→                phase_result = PhaseResult(\n  1099→                    phase=phase,\n  1100→                    status=status,\n  1101→                    exit_code=exit_code,\n  1102→                    started_at=started_at,\n  1103→                    finished_at=finished_at,\n  1104→                    output_bytes=monitor.state.output_bytes,\n  1105→                    error_bytes=error_bytes,\n  1106→                    last_task_id=monitor.state.last_task_id,\n  1107→                    files_changed=monitor.state.files_changed,\n  1108→                )\n  1109→                sprint_result.phase_results.append(phase_result)\n  1110→\n  1111→                debug_log(\n  1112→                    _dbg,\n  1113→                    \"phase_complete\",\n  1114→                    phase=phase.number,\n  1115→                    status=status.value,\n  1116→                    exit_code=exit_code,\n  1117→                    duration=round(_phase_dur, 1),\n  1118→                )\n  1119→\n  1120→                # Log and notify\n  1121→                logger.write_phase_result(phase_result)\n  1122→                notify_phase_complete(phase_result)\n  1123→\n  1124→                tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, None)\n  1125→\n  1126→                # Decide: continue or halt?\n  1127→                if status.is_failure:\n  1128→                    # Collect diagnostics for the failed phase\n  1129→                    try:\n  1130→                        collector = DiagnosticCollector(config)\n  1131→                        bundle = collector.collect(phase, phase_result, monitor.state)\n  1132→                        classifier = FailureClassifier()\n  1133→                        bundle.category = classifier.classify(bundle)\n  1134→                        reporter = ReportGenerator()\n  1135→                        diag_path = (\n  1136→                            config.results_dir / f\"phase-{phase.number}-diagnostic.md\"\n  1137→                        )\n  1138→                        reporter.write(bundle, diag_path)\n  1139→                        debug_log(\n  1140→                            _dbg,\n  1141→                            \"diagnostic_report\",\n  1142→                            phase=phase.number,\n  1143→                            category=bundle.category.value,\n  1144→                            path=str(diag_path),\n  1145→                        )\n  1146→                    except Exception as _diag_exc:\n  1147→                        debug_log(\n  1148→                            _dbg,\n  1149→                            \"diagnostic_error\",\n  1150→                            phase=phase.number,\n  1151→                            error=str(_diag_exc),\n  1152→                        )\n  1153→\n  1154→                    sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.HALTED\n  1155→                    sprint_result.halt_phase = phase.number\n  1156→                    break\n  1157→\n  1158→            finally:\n  1159→                shutil.rmtree(isolation_dir, ignore_errors=True)\n  1160→\n  1161→        # Merge preflight results with main-loop results in original phase order.\n  1162→        # Build a lookup from phase number → PhaseResult, main-loop results win\n  1163→        # on conflict (they are the authoritative executor record for claude phases).\n  1164→        _merged: dict[int, PhaseResult] = {r.phase.number: r for r in preflight_results}\n  1165→        for r in sprint_result.phase_results:\n  1166→            _merged[r.phase.number] = r\n  1167→        sprint_result.phase_results = [\n  1168→            _merged[p.number] for p in config.active_phases if p.number in _merged\n  1169→        ]\n  1170→\n  1171→        # Sprint finished\n  1172→        sprint_result.finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n  1173→        if sprint_result.outcome == SprintOutcome.SUCCESS:\n  1174→            # Verify all phases actually passed\n  1175→            if not all(r.status.is_success for r in sprint_result.phase_results):\n  1176→                sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.ERROR\n  1177→\n  1178→        tui.update(sprint_result, MonitorState(), None)\n  1179→        logger.write_summary(sprint_result)\n  1180→        notify_sprint_complete(sprint_result)\n  1181→\n  1182→    finally:\n  1183→        # Ensure monitor thread and subprocess are cleaned up even on exception.\n  1184→        # Each step is independent so one failure does not prevent others.\n  1185→        try:\n  1186→            monitor.stop()\n  1187→        except Exception:\n  1188→            pass\n  1189→        if proc_manager is not None:\n  1190→            try:\n  1191→                proc_manager.terminate()\n  1192→            except Exception:\n  1193→                pass\n  1194→        try:\n  1195→            tui.stop()\n  1196→        except Exception:\n  1197→            pass\n  1198→        try:\n  1199→            signal_handler.uninstall()\n  1200→        except Exception:\n  1201→            pass\n  1202→\n  1203→    # best-effort; do not mask the real exit\n  1209→\n  1210→    if _exitcode != 0:\n  1211→        raise SystemExit(_exitcode)\n  1212→\n  1213→\n  1214→def _classify_from_result_file(\n  1215→    result_file: Path,\n  1216→    started_at: float,\n  1217→) -> PhaseStatus | None:\n  1218→    \"\"\"Classify phase outcome from the agent-written result file.\n  1219→\n  1220→    Returns a PhaseStatus if the result file exists, is fresh (mtime > started_at),\n  1221→    and contains a recognizable EXIT_RECOMMENDATION.
